#!/bin/sh
# shar:	Shell Archiver  (v1.22)
#
#                                                                          
#                                                                          
#
#	Run the following text with /bin/sh to create:
#	  README
#	  adptvisa.dat
#	  airaccid.dat
#	  basesal.dat
#	  baskball.dat
#	  birthrt.dat
#	  caco2.dat
#	  calibrat.dat
#	  cars93.dat
#	  cdrate.dat
#	  chondrit.dat
#	  diabetes.dat
#	  elusage.dat
#	  ethanol.dat
#	  galaxy.dat
#	  gascons.dat
#	  geyser.dat
#	  hckshoot.dat
#	  jantemp.dat
#	  marathon.dat
#	  mbagrade.dat
#	  mbasalry.dat
#	  mbasurv.dat
#	  mineacci.dat
#	  mineexpl.dat
#	  newscirc.dat
#	  quake.dat
#	  racial.dat
#	  safewatr.dat
#	  salary.dat
#	  salmon.dat
#	  salyear.dat
#	  schlvote.dat
#	  sulfate.dat
#	  swissmon.dat
#	  vineyard.dat
#	  votfraud.dat
#	  whale.dat
#
if test -r s2_seq_.tmp
then echo "Must unpack archives in sequence!"
     next=`cat s2_seq_.tmp`; echo "Please unpack part $next next"
     exit 1; fi
sed 's/^X//' << 'SHAR_EOF' > README &&
X                     File README
X                     -----------
X
Xsmoothmeth  A collection of the data sets used in the book "Smoothing
X            Methods in Statistics," by Jeffrey S. Simonoff,
X            Springer-Verlag, New York, 1996. Submitted by Jeff
X            Simonoff (jsimonoff@stern.nyu.edu).
X
X
XThis submission consists of 37 files, plus this README file.
XEach file represents a data set analyzed in the book.
XThe names of the files correspond to the names given in
Xthe book. The data files are written in plain ASCII (character)
Xtext. Missing values are represented by "M" in all data files.
X
XSeveral of the files include an alphabetic (labeling) variable. It is
Xlikely that these files would have to be input into a package using fixed,
Xrather than free, format. The relevant files, along with appropriate
XFortran format statements, are as follows:
X
X   adptvisa.dat: (f10.4,4x,f7.4,3x,a20)
X
X   airaccid.dat: (i3,3x,a34)
X
X   basesal.dat : (f8.1,4x,a17)
X
X   baskball.dat: (f7.4,4x,f6.4,3x,i3,4x,f5.2,3x,i2,3x,a17)
X
X   cars93.dat  : (f5.1,2x,i2,2x,i2,3x,f3.1,2x,i3,3x,f4.1,2x,i4,2x,a21)
X
X   elusage.dat : (i4,3x,f7.3,2x,a7)
X
X   hckshoot.dat: (f7.3,4x,i1,4x,a20)
X
X   jantemp.dat : (i6,3x,a30)
X
X   marathon.dat: (f10.2,4x,a27)
X
X   newscirc.dat: (f8.2,3x,f7.2,2x,a25)
X
X   racial.dat  : (f7.4,4x,a32)
X
X   safewatr.dat: (i5,3x,i3,3x,a26)
X
X   schlvote.dat: (i3,4x,f5.2,2x,i8,4x,f4.1,5x,f5.2,2x,i7,2x,a25)
X
XDescription of data sources, and further information about the data sets,
Xcan be found in the "Descriptions of the data sets" section of the book.
XPointing a World Wide Web browser to the URL
X
X            http://www.stern.nyu.edu/SOR/SmoothMeth
X
Xwill provide access to a site devoted to the book.
X
XNOTICE: These datasets may be used freely for scientific,
Xeducational and/or non-commercial purposes, provided suitable
Xacknowledgment is given (by citing the reference above).
X
SHAR_EOF
chmod 0755 README || echo "restore of README fails"
sed 's/^X//' << 'SHAR_EOF' > adptvisa.dat &&
